Mr. Moon Sun-myung's Selected Words
72
Compilation Committee of Mr. Moon Sun-myung's Words

Foreword
                   President of the World Peace Unification Family Association  Hwang  Seon-jo

1)
A World That Exists for Others
Dear esteemed teachers, I sincerely thank you for the opportunity to meet you here after waiting for so long. 
Human beings find joy through what they eat and see. Today, we are enjoying food and various environments, but I ask you to also give a round of applause to those who have provided us with music, songs, and piano performances. (Applause)
God has loved this Japan more than any other country.
I believe that many of you may have various doubts about Moon Sun-myung as the founder of the Unification Church. I am the person referred to as Moon Sun-myung, and I hope you will judge me well. I love all of you esteemed teachers from the bottom of my heart.
No matter how old or outdated something is in human history, in front of God, who is an eternal and unchanging being, it is new and merely a momentary existence. From this perspective, the country of Japan, as the Japanese people desire, has been loved by God more than anyone else.
On May 7, 1974 (Tuesday), at the Imperial Hotel (Tokyo, Japan).
* This speech was given at a banquet attended by over 1,700 prominent figures from Korea, China, Japan, and others, known as the Day of Hope, and is also published in the "Collection of Speeches by Mr. Moon Sun-myung" and the July 1974 issue of "Unification World."
8   A World That Exists for Others
I believe that God has loved this Japanese archipelago more than anyone else. (Applause)
The fact that this Japanese archipelago has established a nation and has been protected until now, especially after World War II, is something that you all know well: there is no other country in world history that has received such blessings. While the efforts of the Japanese people played a role, it goes without saying that behind it all, there has been God's protection, blessing, and love.
In this land of Japan, the city of Tokyo is the center of Japan, and God, who has loved Japan, cannot help but love Tokyo, the capital of Japan, and the citizens of Tokyo. Among the citizens, those who are most loved are the esteemed teachers who have come here today. When I think of this, it is needless to say that God loves you deeply. I consider it an immense honor that so many esteemed teachers have gathered here this evening to welcome me, who is lacking. I sincerely thank the representatives from Korea and the Republic of China for attending this banquet. (Applause)
Korea, Japan, and the Republic of China are all brothers in the land of Asia. If these brothers unite and strive to give a love greater than what Japan has received from God, that is, to extend God's higher love beyond Japan to Asia or the world, and if we can all hold hands and move forward with a brotherly heart in that direction, I believe this evening can be a turning point, and there would be nothing more joyful than that.
Human beings are relative beings who can achieve God's love, happiness, and ideals.
I wish for God's deep protection to be with you in your lives, families, and this society, and I would like to share my thoughts from now on.
9 
Throughout human history, in every era, people have pursued a world of eternal, universal, and true love, happiness, peace, and ideals. Even in modern times, we are waiting and striving for this to be realized. However, we are all too aware that we stand in a place where the hope of this being achieved is lacking. Therefore, people become discouraged and feel that "this world has come to an end. We cannot go any further," and we know that they are suffocating under such limitations.
In this changing world of humanity, even if such hope is not realized, if there exists an absolute God beyond humanity, that God will surely fulfill true love, true peace, true happiness, and true ideals. There is no other path for us to pursue.
When we think about it this way, God Himself must be the King of Love, or the King of Peace and Happiness, and the center of ideals. Therefore, when humans pursue such things and hit a limit, I believe there is no other way to break through except through God.
When we think about love, happiness, peace, and ideals, we realize that these cannot be achieved by a single person. Without a relationship of reciprocity, love, happiness, peace, and ideals cannot be realized. When we consider this, can God Himself achieve love, happiness, peace, and ideals solely by Himself? If we continue to ask this question, we must conclude that even God cannot achieve it alone. Thus, in order to realize the ideals of reciprocal relationships, someone in this universe must stand in the position of the other.
When we think about this, if God is the subject in this universe, then the only ones who can stand in the position of the relative are us humans. Therefore, the completion of the love that God desires is not achieved by God's love alone, nor is God's peace, happiness, or ideals achieved solely by God Himself; it cannot be accomplished without us humans. (Applause) I feel that until now, no one has thought this deeply about all of humanity or individuals.
If we come to this conclusion, we must recognize that each one of us is a great counterpart to God and that we must restore that value once again. We must rediscover this. We feel that this determination is present here. Therefore, in order to achieve such ideals of reciprocal relationships, it is established that someone in this universe must stand in the position of the other.
Humans can stand in a superior position to God as the subject.
If God is eternal, unchanging, unique, and absolute, it is only natural to desire that the counterpart who achieves that ideal is also eternal and unchanging. Thus, we can conclude that our human pursuit of true love, true happiness, and true ideals throughout history until today has ultimately been a preparation to welcome the subject, God. If we humans stand in such a position, and if God is the embodiment of eternal life, then we must also be relative beings of eternal life.
When we think about this, we must seek the value of humanity to such an extent.
Now, I would like to pose a question to you esteemed teachers. Among you, there seem to be many seniors in age compared to me, but if you were asked when you were young whether you would seek a wife who is better than you or one who is inferior, I believe everyone would have said they want someone better than themselves. That is only natural.
Then, where does such a nature come from? Humans are not the cause of the universe. We cannot deny that we are ultimately beings of results. From this perspective, we come to understand that we humans are result beings derived from some causal existence. Therefore, if we humans have such aspirations, we can think that the original being or the subject that causes this must also have such aspirations. So, if we were to ask God, "God, if you were to establish your counterpart, would you want a counterpart better than yourself or one that is not as good?" then God would have to respond in the same way that humans living on this earth would respond.
God Himself also desires a counterpart that is better than Himself. If not, God could not eternally love humans as counterparts of hope, happiness, or ideals. When we think this way, we can conclude that humans, who can stand in a superior position to God, are of great value.
Another question I would like to pose is this: let’s say a handsome man and a beautiful woman become a wonderful couple. And let’s say they have their first child. The mother holding the child is truly a beautiful woman. When the mother looks at the child, although it is small compared to her and the father, it resembles them. If the husband were to say, "This child is truly beautiful. The child's face is far better than either the father's or the mother's," the mother would smile. However, conversely, if the father were to say, "Absolutely not. That cannot be. My face is much better than the child's," I believe there would be no such father. What do you think? (Applause) It is undoubtedly true.
Originally, we humans were created as the sons and daughters of God. We were born as God's beloved true sons and daughters. Yet, such sons and daughters have become miserable. It is indeed tragic that we live in a world of fallen rights or lamentation. God cannot be pleased to see such a state. We were created as the highest beings in harmony, yet why has it resulted in such a state? From a religious perspective, it is because of the fall. Something has gone wrong. We have fallen to the ground. For some reason, we have become separated from one another.
It is because of this that humanity has become so miserable. However, miserable humanity does not remain in a miserable state; it seeks to transcend this, to go beyond history, and to return to the original homeland of humanity. This is the process we are in. However, that goal has not yet been achieved.
If we think about this, humanity itself must become more precious than God. I hope that you all, having come here, will remember for the rest of your lives, "I heard such words from a person named Moon." (Applause) Considering this outcome, it ultimately leads to the issue of humans standing in the position of the counterpart to the subject, God.
The principle of the ideal of cosmic creation is to exist for others.
God is the King of Wisdom and the Almighty who knows everything, so the true love, true happiness, true peace, and true ideals of the human world must be determined in the direction centered on the subject and the relationship with the object. God must make this decision while looking at the eternal ideal world.
If it becomes centered on God and serves only the subject, and if humans create such traditional standards, and if everything must revolve around and serve the self, then a great problem will arise. In such a position, the principles of unity, fusion, or development cannot be fulfilled.
Thus, we come to understand that it is not the object that serves the subject, but rather that God Himself must take the position of existing centered on the object. When that happens, everything becomes one. Everything follows the principle of development, so the omnipotent God had to establish the standard of the source of peace, happiness, ideals, and love as "to exist for others."
Therefore, ideals, love, peace, and happiness are not to be governed or served by the subject, but rather to be positioned in a way that asks, "For what do we live? For what do we gain?" Only then does true love, true happiness, true peace, and true ideals begin. This is how the principles of the ideal of cosmic creation have been established.
The origin of all existence lies in serving others.
When we think about this, the esteemed teachers here are standing in a subjective position centered on themselves, freely and without any deficiencies. I believe they are wonderful individuals.
When we consider the male teachers, we must think about why men were created. Men were not born centered on themselves. We must not forget that the motivation for the existence of men lies in women. (Applause) However, some may respond, "Well, Mr. Moon, isn't that an unpleasant thing for a man to hear?" Perhaps that is because they have never thought about such things before. However, I hope you do not think of it as an unpleasant thing.
I will continue to speak, but if a man thinks, "I was born for myself," then that notion contradicts the principles of the universe. Women may also think they were born centered on themselves. However, that becomes problematic. Women were not born centered on themselves; they were born centered on men. Therefore, we must recognize here that the origin of existence lies in serving others, and we must live for that.
If a man and a woman who wish to live for others become a couple, then such a couple is indeed an ideal couple. (Applause) Is that not so? Such a couple can seek the true standard of peace. In such a couple, true happiness can be established. Such a couple can become the subject of true love that is eternal and universal.
Then, what kind of parent would truly be an ideal parent when applying these principles? A parent who believes they were born for their children and have existed for their children, rather than existing for themselves and living their lives for themselves. If there are parents who are willing to dedicate their lives and sacrifice everything for their children, then such parents must be true parents. (Applause) These parents are the true peace, true happiness, and true ideals of parenthood. On the other hand, if children believe they were born for their parents, live for their parents, and die for their parents, then those children cannot help but be filial. They will inevitably become children who can receive true love, true happiness, and true peace.

The teachings of all religions also emphasize existing for others. 
If we apply the principle of existing for others centered around a nation, and if we are asked who the greatest patriot in that nation is, an immediate answer comes to mind. For example, if we ask who can be most praised in Japanese history, we might mention General Nogi Maresuke. He dedicated his life to Emperor Meiji and sacrificed everything for Japan when it faced a great crisis. Because he devoted his life and everything he had for Japan, he is undoubtedly a patriot.

If we expand this to apply it to human history, we can ask who the true saints in history are. By applying the principle of existing for others, we can easily identify them. In this light, we cannot help but elevate Jesus Christ as the greatest saint. He came for humanity, lived for humanity, and sacrificed everything for humanity while even blessing his enemies. 

There is no one else who died with the spirit of existing for others, not just for the good but also for the evil. In this regard, we must say that he is the saint of saints. Because Christianity stood in such a position, it has received God's protection, God's love, and has been able to lead culture globally. This is an undeniable reality. If individuals, nations, and the world uphold the principle of existing for others, humanity will surely create a paradise on earth.

I, standing here, have received God's calling and have come to understand the circumstances of the spiritual world. Many teachers may not know much about the spiritual world. However, I have experienced everything about that world. When analyzing that world, we can discover that its structure and organizational system are built upon the principle of existing for others. Therefore, I hope that many teachers will believe that the place where those who exist for others and dedicate their lives goes is heaven.

Thus, the numerous religious scriptures have taught about God centered on the principle of existing for others. For those who seek the heavenly kingdom and are connected to it, it is inevitable that they will educate with content that responds to that standard. Therefore, the higher the religion, the more it emphasizes "Serve and sacrifice." From this principle, it is an entirely natural outcome.

The 66 books of the Bible can all be seen as converging on the single phrase of existing for others. It can be said that it is limited to this one phrase. When we read the words of Jesus in the Bible, they contain content that today's young people cannot even imagine. There are many contradictory statements. It says that those who wish to be exalted will be humbled, and those who wish to be humbled will be exalted. It states that those who wish to lose their life will save it, and those who seek to save their life will lose it. Everything is reversed. Furthermore, although Jesus came as the Savior, he said he did not come to be served but to serve. Everything is contrary. I believe that Jesus taught this because he experienced the deep and profound principles of God.

When we think this way, the teachers present here can easily discern how to distinguish between good and evil people. Those who live for others are undoubtedly good people, while those who seek to exist centered on themselves are in opposition to God's ideal world and are connected to evil. We must discern this fact here.

What is the fall, then? When we examine the content of the Bible, we find that the fall originates from the moment self-awareness began, when one could not exist for the subject, God, and instead thought of oneself as the subject. In other words, the fall was caused by the realization of self and the focus on oneself. Even though one was in the position of existing to serve, the origin of the fall arose from the position of existing centered on oneself.

The Bible shows that Eve caused Adam to fall. The woman caused the man to fall. Who did she do it for? To protect herself, she abandoned the principle of existing for others and sought to center everything around herself, which led to the fall. This became the beginning of the world of evil. Our ancestors produced such results from that evil position. Because we were born as descendants of such ancestors, humanity today thinks of everything centered on itself.

Initially, people think of themselves first. This is a gift of the consequences brought by the fall. God cannot simply overlook such a world. We must reclaim the good world. The movement to reclaim the good world must be carried out through history, and that is religion. (Applause)

If this is the truth, when we discover that such achievements have been left in human history, we come to know that God moves history. We can conclude that God must exist, and this is a just conclusion. (Applause)

Why did God establish the principle of existing for others? Wouldn't it have been fine not to establish such a principle? Some may think this way. If so, let me pose a question here. 

When we analyze our true intentions, it is evident that our true intentions are in a good position. If someone were to risk their life for themselves or have a heart of 100% sacrificial love to bring happiness to themselves, would there be someone who, from that 100% standard, would take 50% for themselves and try to return only 50%? Surely everyone would answer that this is not possible. 

In truth, this heart is a wonderful heart. Because of such a nature, when one receives 100% love, they want to return even more than that. That is why, even though humanity has fallen, we can still have the hope of returning to our original world. Why is that? Because if I give 100 to a person named B, that person will return more than 100 to me. That return will be sincere. In that case, I will also be in a position to repay, and I must return more than 120%. If I return to B, it will inevitably conclude that I will receive more than 120% back. Thus, through the interaction between the subject and the object, the concept of eternity is established.

Therefore, we conclude that God had to establish the principle of existing for others in pursuit of eternity. (Applause) From this, development comes. Prosperity arises. Reproduction can occur. That is why ordinary parents teach their children to do good. They say, "Good deeds are such and such. Serve and sacrifice for others. If you serve the whole, blessings will come, and you will become great." 

Even if they do not fully understand the content, we can see that they say such things because they acknowledge that the principles of the universe are structured that way. 

On the other hand, God could not help but establish the principle of existing for others in the following way. If such a standard is not established, a center cannot be established. A person who sacrifices their life with the heart of existing for others will inevitably become a central figure as the sun and moon change.

For example, let’s say there is a family of ten people. There are parents, older brothers, and sisters. If the youngest sibling dedicates their entire being for the family, naturally, the parents will center around that child. It goes without saying that not only the parents but also the older siblings will center around the youngest sibling. Thus, we can recognize the ironclad principle that those who wish to exist for others become the center.

Once a center is determined, the entire family will automatically want to receive their guidance. Even if they do not wish to, everyone will want that person to become the center of the household. 

In human society, being guided may be seen as shameful, but truly, people want to receive guidance from those who work hard for others. We cannot help but acknowledge that there is no greater happiness than this.

If God, the center of the universe, exists for the universe, then the happiness we receive from being guided will be unparalleled. Therefore, if we cannot find the standard by which God can exist, we cannot automatically fill the ideal realm with the determination of the center. That is why God had to establish the principle of existing for others.

Another point is that our desire is to value love and ideals more than life and to want to grasp them in our hands. 

Until now, people have thought that love and ideals could be obtained through themselves. However, that is absolutely not the case. Love is never one's own. Ideals are also not one's own. Love is not achieved by oneself but is given by the counterpart, and this is a principle. Ideals are also not achieved by oneself but are obtained from the counterpart. Therefore, to accept that love and ideals, which are more precious than life, one must exist to serve. (Applause)

Religious unity becomes possible when the principle of existing for others is upheld. 
When we consider this principle, we can only fulfill true love, true happiness, and true ideals by existing for others. This principle is established in the lives of all teachers and in every society and world.

The person standing here, named Moon, has given the name "World Christian Unity Association" to the church I established. Is unity truly possible? It will undoubtedly happen. But will it really happen?

Even within Christianity, there have been over 400 denominations that have historically fought against each other. You all know this is an undeniable fact. Christianity itself is already in a stage of collapse. At this stage, you may wonder what the Unification Church is, and you might think that Mr. Moon is a bit out of his mind. However, I do not think it is that difficult.

If there is a denomination that holds the principle of existing for others, and if all denominations strive beyond that, then they will surely become one. Even if it is a different religion, if that religion can exert efforts beyond the spirit it advocates, I believe that religion can also become one. I, as a human, may not be able to do it, but because God is such a being, and because the subject God is such a being, I believe that if we maintain that relative position, we will naturally become one through God's power. This is logical.

Therefore, becoming one is not such a difficult task. The Unification Church began on this principle. The Unification Church has faced various problems in Japan, and I believe that many teachers present here have harbored doubts and criticisms about this organization and this church. However, the Unification Church has never once made excuses. The truth is not recognized by humans or by propaganda but is recognized through substantial results. (Applause)

This person standing here has been persecuted in Korea for decades. I have been rejected from various fields, by individuals, families, numerous religions, and even by national sovereignty. However, I have never made excuses. Why? Because God is like that. I know God, who, while sacrificing His most beloved, does not seek compensation or make excuses.

To be someone who can follow that one who exists for others, one must walk silently. And because the path is busy, there is no time to care about the noisy surrounding environment. In that position, I have lived and worked until now.

The more one exists for others, the more they become the master. 
The Unification Church has been beaten and trampled but has not fallen. In the meantime, we have built a global foundation. The loud proclamations made in America were based on this content. I warned that individualism would perish. No matter how much America leads the world, if a religious organization arises that loves the country of America more than the American people themselves, then America will be dominated by that religion. 

Why is that? Because God is such a being; if one truly acts with such love, everything will be subject to that love. This is a fact. 

The same goes for you in Japan. Who is the master of Japan? It must be someone who loves the Japanese people and the Japanese nation more than anyone else. This is an undeniable principle. Then, whose is the universe? The universe must belong to the one who loves the universe more than anyone else.
If there is only one way to occupy God, it is to serve God beyond what humanity has been able to do throughout history up to today. If a person who exists for God is born, then through that person, the world and God's world can establish an essential path. We believe that the one who comes to do such work is the Messiah. (Applause)

In thinking this way, I feel very sorry that our Unification Church has caused considerable problems in Japan. Young people are gathering and shouting that they will save Japan and the world. They may say that the era of only serving Japan has passed. If Japan had truly waged the Greater East Asia War for Asia, such a miserable outcome would not have occurred. If it had genuinely been for Asia, what would Japan be like today? Surely, it would have become the leader of Asia.

Therefore, we must consider the principles of the universe. From the moment you meet a person named Moon (문) here, if you apply these principles in personal relationships, friendships, or in the relationship between a company president and subordinates, you will surely prosper. It will continue infinitely. It will flourish greatly. Such a person will naturally become a central figure, and everyone will want to receive guidance from that person forever. Society, nations, and peoples will want to be guided by such a person.

When that happens, hearts will connect, and a nation of love will be established. Only when hearts connect can a nation be guided. If a nation becomes such a nation, then the country where such people live will be the ideal nation.

We must establish America to save the world. 

Looking at history, it can be said that it is a history stained by dictators, individualism, and selfishness. Therefore, someone must develop a movement to preserve a history contrary to this and to clean up history. If God exists, He would naturally desire such things.

Our Unification Church is currently carrying out such a movement, even if no one acknowledges it from the ends of the world. That is why young people from Japan are going to America to engage in activities. Japan is in a very busy era, facing the fate of confronting the Communist Party, and there is a reality that we must change and organize this into a new direction. Why are we going to America to work instead of returning to Japan? Some people say we should be active in Japan. However, that is not the case.

Right now, America is undoubtedly the country leading the world of democracy. If this country were to perish, it would become a global issue. The only country defending communism is America. Many teachers are well aware that Japan itself cannot do that right now.

Current Japan can be likened to a naked woman. China is rushing to marry her. Meanwhile, the Soviet Union is also proposing marriage. Until now, Japan had been holding hands with the gentleman called America, but now it has rejected that and pulled away. It goes without saying that Japan, in such a position, cannot lead the world.

From this perspective, although Japan's reality is urgent, to save the world, we must establish America. Establishing America is the most difficult task. Who is willing to take responsibility and dedicate their life to such work?

I have waited long and searched through countless religions and religious people. I have met many local council members and famous figures. I have met all the notable people in that country. However, in their hearts, there was no thought of saving the world. Even during the Watergate incident, if things had slipped even slightly, America could have fallen to the bottom. Numerous religious leaders or globally renowned figures like Billy Graham should have been at the forefront of the nation, leading a movement to prevent that, but they were not even thinking about it in their dreams. Thus, the person named Moon, born in a corner of the East, took on that responsibility. (Applause)

However, this is not something that can be done carelessly. I have risked my life to negotiate with God to find out what He desires. The person standing here is not a politician. I am someone who acts according to God's words. Someone must speak up to protect the country, protect the world, and indicate the direction to go. Because I understood that, I was prepared for a path of adventure. The Unification Church has established the era that the whole world has built through blood and sweat, and has made the final decision.

Young people of unity working in the enemy's country for Asia and the world.

I told President Nixon that if we could endure well from mid-March to the end of April, everything would be resolved. That is how it is. Why is that? It is because I felt that it would be resolved. Standing in the right position, if we do not repent for our mistakes and bravely overcome them, there is no way to save America from the national crisis. It seems that no one has said such things.

Thus, we have taken on the most difficult task in America. However, there are not enough people. We are lacking in numbers. There are only a few thousand members of the Unification Church in America. With such a small number, we cannot move America. Therefore, we urgently mobilized nearly a thousand young people from about 11 countries. This has now become a major issue.

This has been publicized, and immigration has become a problem.

The work being done by the Unification Church is wonderful. The youth of the Unification Church are desirable people not only in Japan but also in America. However, from a legal standpoint, they cannot engage in fundraising or business with tourist visas, so they are in violation of the law. However, even if they are in violation of the law, if they step forward for America more than the American people, they do not violate God's law. That is why we took the risk. All the major issues that arose from such activities were for America.

From the perspective of Japanese youth, America is the enemy country from World War II. The same goes for the youth of Germany. That is why I brought the most young people from Japan and Germany to America. Why? Because if Japanese and German people come to love America more than their own countries in the enemy country of America, a new transnational nation can be born here.

Someone must set such a goal and work for the entire world. When young people from Japan transcend Japan and accomplish such work in America, it cannot be anything but a source of pride for Japan. From a historical standpoint, the relationship between Japan and America is very complex. However, if what they are doing now leaves a mark in history, it will become a motive to unite Japan and America in the future.

With this goal in mind, young people in Japan are now stepping forward to work for the construction of a "world that exists for others." I believe this is a source of pride not only for those present here but for all Japanese people. (Applause)

And it is about uniting the people of Korea, Japan, and the Republic of China in America. If we begin to influence the East and start moving while knowing America, there may be a way for Japan to be saved. Considering the current situation of the Republic of China and the Republic of Korea, I believe that there is no way to regenerate the urgent Asia that is being pushed by the communist bloc other than seeking such a path.

When I think that young people in Japan are fighting for not only the current issues but also the future of Asia with such determination, I felt I had to convey this content to many teachers. I sincerely hope that many teachers will unite with the young people who are working for Asia and the world. Then the country will prosper. If such a country and such an Asian sphere are established, it will become Asia that leads the world centered around the new ideal sphere of Asia.

At a time when the world is plunged into chaos and heading towards darkness, if there is a group that sacrifices everything, takes risks, and moves transnationally with the determination to "exist for others," God cannot help but be with such a group. I believe it will be a group that can build the ideal world pursued throughout history.

I hope that all of you will consider that the person named Moon standing here is active with such thoughts. I wish to live the remainder of my life with such principles until I die.

To exist for others is a command of the philosophy of the universe and the principle of the original source of the universe.

In conclusion, I want to say that individuals must sacrifice for their families. This is a command of the universal principles. It is through such people that families will be saved. Families must sacrifice for clans, clans for nations, and nations must sacrifice everything for the world. If there is a nation that exists for others, that nation will be saved. Nations must dedicate everything to their countries. They must serve. They must sacrifice. Then such a nation will never perish. Moreover, we must not stop at that nation. We must sacrifice beyond that nation. This is because God is not the God of one nation.

God is the God of all nations. He is the one who wants to establish the world as one family, as one nation. Therefore, unless the idea arises that we must save the world even at the cost of sacrificing our nation, there will be no way to make the world one. We must stand in a transnational position.

The Soviet Union had the idea of world domination centered around the Slavic people. That became the motive for the breakdown of relations with China. (Applause) America is also leading the world based on democracy. However, America must not stand in a position of world domination prioritizing itself. We must save the world even at the cost of America. If we become such a nation, even if the land and the people disappear, if a culture remains that has done such things, that culture will dominate the world. This is the most important thing. In the current Asia, if there is a movement to unite by sacrificing their own countries to block the global organization of communism, this Asia will never perish. If the continents unite across six continents for the world, I believe the world will not perish.

Therefore, individuals must live for their families, families for clans, clans for nations, nations for the world, and the world for one world. Only such men and women can become the children of God, the subject of the universe. Those who only love their own country cannot become the children of God.

God governs world history centered on saints who can lead the world and live for the world. Therefore, establishing religions and cultural spheres could not have been done without that principle. (Applause)

In a word, this principle is "to exist for others." And this principle is the principle of the original source of the universe. When we consider that this principle is the foundation of ideals, we can only find all happiness, all peace, all ideals, and all love by standing on that principle.

Let us mobilize for Asia and the world and pioneer the ideal world.

Knowing this principle makes education for children very simple. When we say "to exist for others," parents themselves must embody that. Teachers must not be those who chase after money. They must be beings who dedicate their lives for their students. When such movements are carried out globally, the ideal world, the "Day of Hope" and "New Day of Hope" that are at stake will be established in the historical process of this planet. (Applause)

I hope that you all, including President Kubo of the Unification Church, will guide these young people, who may have various shortcomings in what they are doing, so that Japan can become a beautiful Japan, a Japan with hope, and a Japan that the world can trust, a Japan that all small nations in Asia can admire.

If Japan becomes a nation that can influence the world, transcending individuals, society, the nation, and all ethnicities with the principle of existing for others, Japan will surely be able to lead the world.

If any small country in Asia establishes and practices this principle, I believe that the world will be guided by that country. Therefore, if we unite and resolve to mobilize for Asia and the world, and each of us makes efforts to pioneer the ideal world from now on, there will be no greater glory than that.

With this thought, I wish for your future health, the happiness of your families, and success in society, while hoping that God's love will be with you, I will conclude my remarks. (Applause)*

**The Whole and I**
Everyone living on this earth considers the concept of "self" to be important. They think of family centered around themselves, think of the nation centered around themselves, think of the world centered around themselves, and eventually think of God as well. This is the nature of humanity. Here, we can find that we are beings who cannot escape the world of relative relationships.

The nation is the fruit of all ancestors.
When we think about where the concept of a nation originated, it started from our ancestors from long ago, from God. We know that human history has passed through hundreds of thousands of years, but it is not an exaggeration to say that this historical connection ultimately came about to weave together one individual, to bring one individual into existence.

Among those ancestors, how many grandmothers and grandfathers must there have been? At times, there would have been tall grandfathers, and at other times, short grandfathers, tall grandmothers, and short grandmothers, and various types of people. If we were to present those ancestors in front of us today, there would be various types of people. There would be beauties, there would be ugly people, there would be disabled people, and there would be all sorts of individuals. As we consider all those ancestors, we can conclude that they cannot help but represent the human image living on this earth today.

Among those ancestors, there would be good people from God's perspective, and there would be bad people. Among the bad people, there would be those who stole others' belongings, and there would be all sorts of people. All the blood of those ancestors mixed together to give birth to your existence. Therefore, we cannot deny that it is not a pure, clean, and beautiful past.

When we look at it this way, if we were to judge whether there were more good people or more bad people among your ancestors, we would have to conclude that there were more bad people than good ones. So, what do you think? Do you think all your ancestors were good people? We cannot deny that they were not. (Laughter) We must understand that today’s "I" was born as the fruit of that whole.

History turns through the four seasons of spring, summer, autumn, and winter.
The fruit is the totality of all the reactions and influences that have passed through the entire year, the 365 days. When you see an apple, if there is a spot on that apple, it did not occur by chance. It was created due to the influences that the apple tree received over the course of a year.

When we look at the existence of "I," the general human tendency is to hope for good and bad centered around oneself. The judgment of "If I like it, it's good, and if I don't like it, it's bad" is a most shameful fact when we consider that we are individuals with a historical background.

Since a person appears as a result of all historical outcomes, even if there were good ancestors in the past, one can still be bad in the present age. When we think about how something can be bad in our time as a historical outcome, it cannot be denied.

Some people rise like this, and some people rise like that. They refuse the center. (While writing on the board) So, is your ancestor one person? Can you say, "I will rise like this"? (Laughter) If we see this, even those who are in the worst positions will judge based on themselves. "Ah, everything should revolve around me..." But what will happen if that is the case?

You revolve around the 365 days of a year through the four seasons of spring, summer, autumn, and winter. From this perspective, you can see a straight line drawn from your ancestors to you, but it can also be thought of as a circular form. If the top is good, then the bottom is bad; if the east is good, then the west is bad. That is why history turns. Even in a day, the morning is like spring, the day is like summer, the evening is like autumn, and the night is like winter. When we see this, there is a fortune that rises centered around noon and a fortune that descends.

In this way, no matter how many ancestors you have, they have all existed within cycles like the spring season, summer season, autumn season, and winter season. Because the figures of the ancestors have been reflected through history, even if we look at this world today in a flat manner, it cannot help but appear in this type.

Therefore, among people, there are those like the spring season, those like the summer season, those like the autumn season, and those like the winter season. Isn’t that true? That is why a person like the spring season should relate to a person like the autumn season, and a person like the summer season should relate to a person like the winter season. Marriage should also be considered from this perspective. Isn’t that right?

From that perspective, if we look at a person's life, there is a boyhood, then a youth, an adulthood, and an old age. When combining my relatives, the people currently present, and your descendants, the question arises: who is the most precious person among the whole? Who is the most excellent ancestor? The ancestor who lived for the whole is the most excellent ancestor.

Your ancestors would want you to do what they could not do through you. Your lineage would hope that through you, it can achieve what it could not. Furthermore, your descendants would wish for you to be an ancestor who accomplishes what no ancestor has done before. Then, what kind of person can those people be proud of? If I want to be the kind of person who stands in that position, what kind of person must I become? This person sitting here must do what the ancestors could not do for the world, for humanity, and through history. Do you understand? "Yes."

The Unification Church exists not for itself but for the world.

Today, all of you gathered here are members of the Unification Church. However, you must understand that among so many people, there are many levels. Let's take a look. It is normal to think that if one is a member of the Unification Church, everyone should be the same. However, you must recognize that there is spring, summer, autumn, and winter here. Just as a year is made up of those seasons, today, not everyone in the Unification Church is working on the front lines. Some work in the rear, some have missions like eyes, some like hands, some like noses; all missions are different. However, as long as everyone is in the position of existing for the whole, that is sufficient. If the eye only sees itself, it is nothing. If the mouth speaks only for itself, it is not for itself. It is for the whole... Ultimately, it is the Unification Church that sees with its eyes. It is the Unification Church that hears with its ears. It is the Unification Church that speaks with its mouth. It is the Unification Church that works with its hands. If it is like that, then regardless of what happens, it will become one. That is normal.

Then, where does the Unification Church itself head towards? It does not head towards itself. It heads towards the world. When this happens, that organization is undoubtedly a true organization. If it continues with this principle for the world eternally, the Unification Church will never perish. Therefore, the Unification Church should not live for itself but for the world. Members of the Unification Church do not live as members of the Unification Church but live for the world. Do you understand? "Yes." If it is an organization that goes like that, it will not perish.

Some may feel uncomfortable thinking, "I am not here. I am not here, am I?" However, you are being sought by the whole. A person who lives for others will inevitably become a central being. A person who is wished to be a central being is someone who lives forever for themselves. All organizations hope that he becomes the president of that country and that he will give for his organization. Therefore, a person who gives will automatically become a central being. God is also such a being. I would like to speak more in detail, but since that is not the topic for today, I will not.

A true representative is someone who lives for ancestors, humanity, descendants, and God.

Now, from that perspective, the question arises: where should "I" be found? Where should it be sought? It should not be sought in oneself. It must be sought in the world. When one finds oneself in the world, that person can emerge as a central being of the world.

When thinking about the concept of "I" and the whole, one must always think, "I am a person who represents my ancestors." First, it means being a representative of the past. Then, in the present, it means being a representative of relatives, this country, and this world. Finally, it means being a representative ancestor for the future descendants, becoming a true ancestor.

Then, what kind of person is a representative? It is a person who sacrifices more for the whole. Right? "Yes." What kind of true representative is it? It is someone who lives for history, lives for the times, and lives for the future. Moreover, it is someone who lives for God. It is someone who lives for God of the past, present, and future. Everyone, don't you want to be that? "I want to." If there is someone who wants to be like that, that person, although currently present, would want to go to the past to boast to the ancestors, to boast to the people of the present world, and to boast to the descendants of the future, right? Do you understand what I mean?

A word through history — Die for the whole.

Therefore, it is not enough to exist for ancestors, humanity, and descendants. If one exists for the historical God, the contemporary God, and the future God, then that person can become a son or daughter who can live forever with God. God is looking for such people. The history of humanity, past, present, and future, is looking for such people. Everyone, do you not want to meet such a person? "I want to." What do you want to do when you meet them? "To become like that person..."

Then, if you have met that person and want to become like that person, what must you do? You must receive education through that person. When receiving education, you must be taught to live for your ancestors, to live for humanity, to live for your descendants, and to live for God's past, present, and future. Do you want to receive such education? "Yes." Ultimately, in one word, it means "Die. Die for the past. Die for the present. Die for the future. Die for God." That is the only way. That is the conclusion in one word. That is why Jesus said, "Those who want to live will die, and those who want to die will live." That is a word through history. Is that a good word? "Yes." Do you welcome that word? "Yes." Then, die. Die. (Laughter) Now, you have answered with your mouths that it is good. You understand.

A person who dedicates their life for their country will forever rule that country, and a person who dedicates their life for humanity will forever rule humanity. A person who dedicates their life for heaven and earth will forever rule humanity. It means becoming a representative and a central figure. From this perspective, a person who has the thought, "I represent my ancestors, I represent humanity, I represent future descendants, and I represent God's past, present, and future," can only be a member of the Unification Church.

"If I exist for heaven and earth more than any ancestor, if I exist for heaven and earth more than any relative or country, if I exist for heaven and earth more than any future descendant, if I labor as long as God labors," then that person can forever become a son of God. If one holds onto this thought forever, you will not experience fatigue when you go out to your local area. It is because this thought is not established that you feel tired.

Everyone, how many years have you lived like this? "One year." Do you want to live just a few years or forever? Then you cannot complain. You cannot even think in your dreams that it is hard. Do you understand? (Laughter) When viewed like this, you must understand that all teachings of human ethics, morality, and religion are based on this background.

If you want to assert yourself, assert yourself from the position of representing the whole.

Parents exist for their children, children exist for their parents, parents exist for their country, and the country exists for the world; a world that supports each other is heaven. Do you want to live in such a world, or do you want to live in a world that supports itself? "In such a world." A person going to hell is someone who lives for themselves, while a person going to heaven is someone who lives for the whole. It is clearly divided. Now, whose is this? It is not yours. It belongs to the universe. You must understand that if it is this country, it belongs to this country; if it is the world, it belongs to the world. I have nothing to assert for myself. Is this eye my eye? "No." It has been received from my ancestors. If the ancestors were to seek everything that resembles them, you would cease to exist. (Laughter) That is not me. You must understand that being me means standing in the position of representing the whole. Therefore, the statement to center around me is valid there.

When you recognize that you are a representative of the whole, it is a valid theory to emphasize myself. At that time, the statement "Be for me," "Honor me," can be made. In that position, it is natural to say, "Let’s stand as the center of the whole." What does that mean? It means not recognizing that I stand as a representative of the whole and not thinking that I am a representative of the whole — that is the principle. When thinking like that, asserting myself and asking to be respected is a fallacy.

To be able to assert myself, it is valid to assert from the position of representing the whole. However, today, we humans do not know this; we forget the whole and assert only ourselves. If we had not fallen, we would have asserted ourselves as representatives of the whole and asked to be respected, but because we have fallen, we deny the whole and center only on ourselves.

God stands in the position of representing the universe, so He can say, "Honor me." God Himself is like that. In such a position, you can assert yourselves as well. Do you understand? "Yes."

So, where do you want to go? To become a center, what must you do? "You must sacrifice." Then, where do you start this work? You start it from here among your family... Now, saying, "Even if there is food, I will eat the delicious one. Even if I wear clothes, I will wear the good ones. Even if I sit, I will sit in the best place. Wherever there is a good place, I will seek that good place," is all wrong. So, from now on, start.

Let’s carry out the commands given by God for the world with gratitude.

You all like to give orders, but you don’t like to receive them, right? "Yes." You must become the opposite, like little children. A person who can receive and carry out the commands of all people can dominate the hearts of all people. They can conquer. The way to conquer God's heart is also that path. To say that I will receive all the commands given by God for the world is the same as saying that I am prepared to die for the world.

Now that you understand, even if the teacher says, "Hey, work day and night, 24 hours, until you die in America," you must say "Yes." For ordinary people, the legal standard is to eat three meals a day and sleep for eight hours, yet the teacher will make you work without feeding or letting you sleep. (Laughter) Even so, will you be grateful? "Yes." If you become like that, God will come dancing to find you. (Laughter) Therefore, do not complain. Do not be discouraged. "Oh, I’m tired. Oh, it’s annoying. I’m exhausted..." But God, who knows everything, who knows human circumstances, will give you points at that time. "Ah, this guy can reject God at this time and betray His will at that time." That is how it will be recorded.

As you live, when you see something that could make you furious, just be grateful and move on. Then see how much joy comes to your heart. Ladies, try this. Even if your pretty faces get tanned and your hair looks like this and you have an unpleasant appearance, if it happened for yourself, it has no value. However, if it happened for God, for the world, and for humanity, it becomes more amazing than the bright morning sunlight.

Now that you are selling flowers and peanuts, there may be times when you cry while trying to catch people on the street. At that time, if you say, "Oh God, how pitiful You must be to see me doing such work to fulfill Your will," how adorable and praiseworthy would that be? But if you say, "Oh God, what is this? I graduated from college and had high dreams; what is this?" then there is a world of difference. It is the same situation, but one is heaven, and the other is hell. That is where hell and heaven are born. Therefore, do not cry for yourself. Do not complain for yourself; complain for heaven. For heaven, it is okay to say, "This world is evil and cannot be." So, you must strive not to get caught in Satan's net.

Now, you should understand "the whole and me." You must know that if the whole is not established, nothing will be accomplished, and you must go for this purpose. Since we have stepped forward representing the world, I hope you will show a bold, brave, and vigorous appearance as warriors of unification who carry the greatest task greater than any organization or historical figure. You must recognize that this is our pride that no organization or country in the world has. Do you understand? "Yes."

<Prayer> Beloved Father, we have designated this training center, Belvedere, which is admired by the unification group of the whole world. It must be a place remembered in Your heart, where Your children moving here will admire Your world of peace and love.

Today, the young children near New York have gathered here at this time, so please embrace their tender kneeling figures, Father. In their hearts, they have a desire to draw an ideal family that You want, and moreover, they are longing for an ideal lineage, an ideal nation, an ideal world, and the world of dreams that You envisioned. Father, knowing this, please look upon them with affection and love.

Although the standard of sons and daughters You desire is high and precious, that position is not achieved dramatically; rather, it must be crossed with the sorrow and pain of fighting in the realistic process of today’s life, with one work, one person, and one environment.

Let us not live for ourselves but for the whole, for the Father, and for the whole nation. May we become children who fight until the end with this concept, creating everything in the world as one with You. May You establish us as people who can proudly boast of ourselves in Your ideal world, and through those boasting sons and daughters, may You be exalted as the Father who can also be boasted of throughout all of history.
I know that your heart desires this, so I earnestly hope and wish that you grant us the connection of children who can be worthy before that heart.  
I sincerely ask that you provide the family of unification scattered across Korea, Japan, and the United States, and the entire world, with a satisfying grace at this time. I hope that the children can realize that they cannot escape from the relationship of this connection, like the 'whole and I' mentioned today, and that they can start to form their worldview from a new perspective. I offer all these words in the name of the True Parents. Amen.

The Purpose of Religion  
You are seeing the teacher for the first time, right? I assume you have many questions and things to say. However, I believe that as you study the principles more and become more broadly aware of the teachings, all the questions you want to ask will be resolved.  
Humans must pursue one purpose.  
Our Unification Church does not have a faith perspective that demands blind belief. All results must theoretically align for them to have practical significance in real life and society. The person standing here has also studied science. Therefore, we do not pursue blind logic.  
If God exists, it is true that God's will cannot be fulfilled apart from human society. This is because God's will is centered on us humans, and it must be fulfilled through humans. Also, since God is absolute, there cannot be two purposes that He aims for. If God were to aim for two purposes, He would not be a unique or unified being. Therefore, it must culminate in one purpose.  
May 26, 1974, (Sunday), Belvedere Training Center.  
* The words following 'the whole and I' were added by the editor.  
Then, what is the standard point or the object of purpose to culminate in one purpose? In this created world, there cannot be such existence apart from humans. If the object of that purpose is humans, then humans themselves must also be able to aim for one purpose theoretically.  
However, when we look at ourselves today, we see that the path we are taking is not one path, but two paths, or even multiple paths. If one God created humans as the highest value beings, then humans should theoretically aim for a common culminating point of God's purpose, but the fact that we are not doing so suggests that there is some complication involved.  
Since in one created world, God's purpose through humans is one, it is a natural conclusion from both perspectives that such a world must be pursued by humans and achieved by God. Therefore, through history today, it is essential for humanity, or for each individual, to aim for one cultural world, one sovereign world, one peaceful world, and one unified world, from this perspective.  
However, when we look at ourselves today, we are not in such a position. If you look at yourselves, you can see that your mind and body are different. Isn't that so?  
"Yes."  
As beings created before one God, it should not be so, but when we see that humans themselves are aiming for two directional purposes, we must acknowledge that there is some complication that has led to this situation.  
Humans, as historical beings, must culminate in two directions, so there are those who want to live centered on a mental standard and those who deny that and want to live centered on a physical standard, like animals, asking, "Where is the conscience?" It is undeniable that these two types of humans create the culture of history.  
Humans have a path that the mind desires and a path that the body desires, and because they go back and forth between these two paths, misery and suffering arise here. If God exists, He cannot simply leave such humans alone. Therefore, it must be that God sees the necessity of adjusting things in one way or another.  
If God exists, would He be closer to the mind or the body? "The mind." That is the same regardless of whom you ask. Therefore, we must consider a method of governing the body centered on the mind.  
Then, if there is Satan, who opposes God and becomes an enemy to God, where will Satan base himself? If God is internal, then Satan fights on the external stage of the body. Humans do not realize that this body and mind have become the battleground of the war between God and Satan throughout human history. (Laughter) Do you understand? "Yes." When the mind says this, the body does that. When have you seen them act as one? Satan is not somewhere else, and God is not somewhere else; my mind is the dwelling place of God, and my body has become the dwelling place of Satan. We must recognize that they are in opposition to each other.  
Therefore, you will feel the struggle between your mind and body several times a day. You may not know where God is, but when you do something that is not right according to your conscience, you immediately know it, saying, "You rascal!" (Laughter) When we see this, if there is a connection of assurance in the world of the mind and if there is a unification in the world of the mind, and if we can connect that to the common aspects of humanity beyond the human world and the national level, then there will be a situation that God can rejoice in.  
Thus, we must establish a higher subject of the world of conscience that the mind desires and carry out a movement that says, "Let all people go to the world." If God exists, He cannot help but desire such a movement.  
On the other hand, Satan says to abandon conscience and everything else and just do what your flesh wants, drink, and act freely. That becomes the boundary between the two worlds. So, where are you? Depending on whether you are above or below the central line, you will be determined to be a good person or a bad person. Where do you want to be? "Above." That is the fundamental desire that everyone has.  
Religion aims to make the mind conquer the body.  
It is concluded that such claims have been made historically and globally without change, which must be religion.  
Therefore, religion has developed even as history changes. No nation or ethnicity has continued for thousands of years without it.  
God cannot help but teach us the way to govern this body by creating such a global situation. When the body does what the mind wants, it immediately returns to God. If people were not created this way, we could see that God's creation was flawed. What does not work is because Satan has taken it as a stronghold.  
If God is the plus of the universe, then we humans are in the position of minus. Also, if our minds are in the plus position centered on God, then our bodies must stand in the position of minus, in a relative position where the body can comply. Thus, they must naturally become one.  
However, what is the problem? It is that another plus has arisen in this body. God is the center of the universe, but the false Satan denies the center and wants to become another center, which is evil. Because of this, plus and plus repel each other. (Laughter) You should not be more interested in the rain than in what I say. (Laughter and applause)  
Now that we humans understand this, we must start a new movement. We must carry out a movement to subdue and govern this body. God cannot help but think of that as well.  
Then, what method should we use? We must restrain the body from doing as it pleases. That is the only method. Therefore, religion says, "Do not do what the body wants! Deny it! Absolutely deny it!" "Do not eat what you want! Do not look at what you want to see! Do not listen to what you want to hear! Do not go where you want to go!" This is the movement of denial that takes place. This is the first principle and first rule of religion. (Laughter)  
Now, who among those who do not want to be someone who can govern the body? Raise your hand among those with a conscience... (Laughter) It concludes that everyone needs religion. (Applause and laughter) It is necessary.  
Everyone has said that religion is necessary. Why? To become one with God. Stopping the struggle between the body and mind is the only way to become one with God, which is why religion is necessary. Therefore, the higher the religion, the more it seeks to sacrifice the body. "Serve! Sacrifice! Live for others!" This is the entirety of religious teaching. There is no religion that tells you to love your body and live for yourself.  
Two methods to subdue and govern the body.  
When we see this, the fact that such struggling humans have made such claims in this world leads us to theorize that there is someone who wants to make humans one. Therefore, we must affirm that God has been with humanity and has influenced our living background.  
If you restrain the body and gradually liberate the mind, the mind will become strong enough to lead the body as it pleases. Once that becomes a habit, that is religion. Do you understand?  
The purpose is not elsewhere. It is right there. That is the purpose. Going to heaven is not the purpose. The purpose is to make this one. We must make this one, and then the path to heaven will open.  
What does that mean? It means, "Let us return to the position of a person who was originally not broken." If we had united around a mind that was not broken, anyone would know what they would do with their life. It is not that you are unaware like you are now. But because this has split...  
You see, even a radio made by humans can reproduce what people say through waves, so humans, the highest creation made by God, cannot fail to hear the words that come from God. Naturally, they will hear it. If God is omnipotent, He does not create beings who can relate to Him in such a way that they do not know.  
Do you want to know that? "Yes."  
This body has been the dung heap of Satan for thousands of years. (Laughter) So how dirty it is. This must be removed. Therefore, the movement to do this is the life of faith and the life of evangelism. If this is not resolved, that is, if the conscience cannot become one with the original mind and if the body cannot become one with the original conscience, one cannot go to heaven. It is not about believing and going to heaven.  
Is that an easy thing or a difficult thing? "It is difficult." How difficult is it? "It is very difficult." Yes, so what should we do? Is it impossible? "No."  
What should we do? It is difficult to become someone who can govern the body and let the mind take control. God knows that as well. Therefore, apart from the way of subduing the body, God wants to teach another way. The struggle occurs because they are similar. Can an adult fight with a baby? They can because they are similar, right? Therefore, another method is to add several times stronger power to the mind so that it can lead the body. Thus, God wants to teach how to open such a path to humans. What is that? It is to pray with sincerity.  
Any being can pray. Because on the day when the mind receives several times stronger power, it can automatically govern the body.  
You see, turning on the electric light does not happen here just by itself. There is a power plant over there, and it connects from there. When an ordinary person is asked where the electricity is, they say it is here. However, the source of electricity is hundreds or thousands of miles away at the power plant. You are in a position where this wire is cut, so you must correct your conscience from a higher perspective. Just like when a frog is electrified, your body will... If that happens, the body will always be governed.  
God cannot help but think of such matters, so it concludes that what religion deals with is prayer and the movement to govern this flesh. Therefore, when we look at historical religions, we can see that God has been working. We cannot say that God does not exist. The Bible says that Jesus taught this as well.  
Do you understand? "Yes." Therefore, you must know that there are no other methods to return to God and unify before the subject of the world of the mind than these two.  
The peaceful unification of the world starts from a heart that is one with God.  
This body of ours is the kingdom of Satan. Therefore, God teaches us, "Conquer yourself. Overcome yourself." Unless you seek the way to become one with yourself, there will absolutely be no peaceful unification in the world. Today, humanity is trying to create unity or a world of peace centered on the democratic world or the communist world, but that is a mistaken thought. You must understand that it is impossible if we do not stop the struggle between our minds and bodies. Even if we create unity externally, if our bodies and minds are fighting internally, it is impossible. Therefore, true peace begins with me.  
Then, where does it start? It starts not from my mind but from a heart that is one with God. Thus, we must control the body. Therefore, humans are ultimately not causal beings, but rather result-oriented beings. Thus, we must be completely one with the fundamental God. However, you are not one with God.  
Cause and effect are one. They cannot be opposites. Even when we look at science today, it is said to be scientific only when the theoretical cause and theoretical effect align.  
From that perspective, your unity must not be from the result but must start from the cause. The historical mission to connect that is what religion is. Now do you know what religion is? "Yes." This is how humans began to split, and as history went on, they could not become one, so they drew a circle to create unity... (The subsequent words were not recorded and cannot be included.)  
6)  
Complete Restoration  
You always think about complete restoration in your heart. You all know well that the term restoration became necessary because of the fall. What caused the fall? It was due to our ancestors, Adam and Eve, that is, because of parents. Therefore, it is a valid conclusion that complete restoration can occur through true parents.  
To achieve complete restoration, one must be reborn through tears of repentance.  
If we look at the origin of the fall, it began through love. We humans, who should receive God's body centered on love, received Satan's body.
We know that what has happened is the Fall. Originally, if Adam and Eve had become the temple of God and united with Him, they would have become one as a couple, and because of that spiritual oneness, sons and daughters centered on God could have emerged from them. 

In John 8:44, Jesus pointed out that our father, the ancestor of humanity, is Satan. Ultimately, what does it mean that we have fallen? It means that humanity has become the temple of Satan and has united with Satan's body, giving birth to Satan's sons and daughters. This is the Fall. In the end, Adam and Eve formed a negative and unjust love by pairing with Satan against God's will, which is what the Fall is.

So, what must we do to achieve complete restoration? True parents must come and give birth to all of you again. Without that path, it is impossible to reach the standard of complete restoration. That is why Nicodemus came to Jesus at night and asked, and Jesus said that unless one is born again, they cannot see the Kingdom of God. It is the same here. Living again after being born again is called resurrection. Therefore, to resurrect, one must be born again.

In this way, we, the descendants of the Fall, cannot resurrect or enter the ideal world without being reborn, which is the core ideology of religion today. You must understand that this is the core ideology that religion must follow.

So, how do we restore? We must create that reality and center on God's words without going in the opposite direction; otherwise, there is no way to be restored. If we have fallen, we must go back up in the opposite direction.

Now, what should you do? If you want to walk the path of complete restoration, you must purify your bloodline. Your bodies have received the blood of Satan. Do you feel that? "Yes." You may understand it conceptually by hearing the words of the Principle, but do you truly feel that the blood of the enemy of God, the enemy of humanity, and the enemy of history is swirling within your bodies? Whose eyes are these? What kind of eyes are they? They are the eyes of Satan. The mouth, the hands, the feet, the entire body...

That is why Christianity speaks of washing away sin. It means to purify. To do that, you must shed a lot of tears. So, you must understand that repentance is necessary. Repentance means to wash away what has been defiled. It means to regret and to fix things. Without shedding tears of repentance, we cannot remove the defiled blood of Satan from our bodies, which is the traditional principle we must understand.

If this body had not become the house of Satan through the bloodline, God's work of restoration would have been completed in an instant. Originally, God should be the Father. However, because humanity was born as the children of Satan, it is extremely difficult to feel God as the Father. If Satan is the North Pole, then God is like the South Pole.

Therefore, the most difficult thing in the world is to deny this bloodline inherited to this day and to find a way to know God, who was not our Father, as our new Father. Otherwise, we cannot return to the Kingdom of Heaven, which is why the way of salvation has been the most difficult throughout history. You must understand that the reason the omniscient and omnipotent God has not completed His work in 6,000 years lies here.

I was born on this earth through Satan, so I am told to deny everything I see and feel. True religion starts from denial. Can you completely deny? Is that an easy thing to do? "No." How difficult is it? "Very." It is more difficult than restoring humanity today, which is why it has taken God 6,000 years.

Let us find the original man and woman who can unite with God.
No matter how mature one is, how many people have felt in such a position that they are the sons and daughters of God, the body of God, and the entire embodiment of God? How many do you think there are? "None." 

Through history, such responsibility has been established as a condition for indemnity... Complete restoration is difficult. By expanding each condition and building a bridge, passing through the 6,000-year stage, one person has emerged who has denied one thing after another, ultimately denying everything. The Messiah concept is waiting for that representative, that central being who has been achieved.

The Bible teaches us to restore centered on God's words, so everything is completely opposite to the world. If it did not teach us the completely opposite path, we could not find the true way to heaven.

Therefore, if the content of the Bible is not like that, it cannot be the true way to heaven. The Bible is like that. "Do not elevate me, but sacrifice me. Be meek and humble." Since Satan's essence is pride, it must go down in the opposite direction to be denied. Satan fell because he sought to elevate himself. The desire to elevate oneself is the essence of Satan.

Next, it has been said that he has dominated. However, he has dominated others illegally. To deny such the essence of Satan, it is said, "Become a servant to others. Be dominated." It is the opposite. Then, "Whoever wants to be high will be brought low, and whoever wants to be low will be raised up."... Then, "Whoever wants to die will live, and whoever wants to live will die."... It is all the opposite. If the world of Satan wants to go this way, it must turn back... It is all the opposite. Do you understand? "Yes."

From this perspective, the Bible is indeed the word of God and can be said to be the only way to cleanse the evil world. And what is the main ideology of the Bible? It is to create a bride and groom. What does that mean? It means to find the original man and woman who are without sin, who have not received the blood of Satan, who can receive the body of God, and who can unite with God.

Ultimately, what is the Fall? It is the descent from Adam and Eve. Therefore, restoration must begin from here, finding the parents. Since it has come down like this, we must find it and go back in. (While writing on the board) We are not looking for the descending Adam and Eve, but the ascending Adam and Eve. This is the bride and groom. Since we have fallen like this, we must go back up in the opposite direction. This is restoration.
